I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Stacked charts with irregular time intervals interpolate incorrectly
## Description

Stacked area charts with irregular time points where some time series have values for all time points and other only for some interpolate without taking the spacing of the time points into account.

## Expected behaviour

When doing linear interpolation across a longer time span with irregularly placed time points, interpolation should work correctly.

## Steps to reproduce

Steps to reproduce the behavior:

1. Open the literacy rate chart in the admin: https://admin.owid.io/admin/charts/2617/edit
2. Change the chart type to stacked area
3. Select only Germany. Between 1750 and 1950, no real values exist.
4. Add France, which has additional values between 1900 and 1950. 
5. Observe that Germany shows a upwards sloping curve - the reason is that the 8 additional points are calculated as if they were spaced evenly (each incrementing by the same amount) even though they are not spaced evenly in time.

## Screenshots

<img width="807" height="570" alt="Image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/4c89bbb9-1b24-4752-a161-7af1da56d734" />


</pr_description>

    71	    default: 0.7,
    72	    focus: 1,
    73	    mute: 0.3,
    74	} as const
    75	
    76	const BORDER_WIDTH = {
    77	    default: 0.5,
    78	    focus: 1.5,
    79	} as const
    80	
    81	@observer
    82	class Areas extends React.Component<AreasProps> {
    83	    @bind placePoint(point: StackedPoint<number>): StackedPlacedPoint {
    84	        const { dualAxis } = this.props
    85	        const { horizontalAxis, verticalAxis } = dualAxis
    86	        return [
    87	            horizontalAxis.place(point.position),
    88	            verticalAxis.place(point.value + point.valueOffset),
    89	        ]
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    // This places a whole series, but the points only represent the top of the area.
    93	    // Later steps are necessary to display them as a filled area.
    94	    @bind placeSeries(
    95	        series: StackedSeries<number>
    96	    ): Array<StackedPlacedPoint> {
    97	        const { dualAxis } = this.props
    98	        const { horizontalAxis, verticalAxis } = dualAxis
    99	
   100	        if (series.points.length > 1) {
   101	            return series.points.map(this.placePoint)
   102	        } else if (series.points.length === 1) {
   103	            // We only have one point, so make it so it stretches out over the whole x axis range
   104	            // There are two cases here that we need to consider:
   105	            // (1) In unfaceted charts, the x domain will be a single year, so we need to ensure that the area stretches
   106	            //     out over the full range of the x axis.
   107	            // (2) In faceted charts, the x domain may span multiple years, so we need to ensure that the area stretches
   108	            //     out only over year - 0.5 to year + 0.5, additionally making sure we don't put points outside the x range.
   109	            //
   110	            // -@marcelgerber, 2023-04-24
   111	            const point = series.points[0]
   112	            const y = verticalAxis.place(point.value + point.valueOffset)
   113	            const singleValueXDomain =
   114	                horizontalAxis.domain[0] === horizontalAxis.domain[1]
   115	
   116	            if (singleValueXDomain) {
   117	                // Case (1)
   118	                return [
   119	                    [horizontalAxis.range[0], y],
   120	                    [horizontalAxis.range[1], y],
   121	                ]
   122	            } else {
   123	                // Case (2)
   124	                const leftX = Math.max(
   125	                    horizontalAxis.place(point.position - 0.5),
   126	                    horizontalAxis.range[0]
   127	                )
   128	                const rightX = Math.min(
   129	                    horizontalAxis.place(point.position + 0.5),
   130	                    horizontalAxis.range[1]
   131	                )
   132	
   133	                return [
   134	                    [leftX, y],
   135	                    [rightX, y],
   136	                ]
   137	            }
   138	        } else return []
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    @computed get placedSeriesArr(): StackedPlacedSeries<number>[] {
   142	        const { seriesArr } = this.props
   143	        return seriesArr
   144	            .filter((series) => !series.isAllZeros)
   145	            .map((series) => ({
   146	                ...series,
   147	                placedPoints: this.placeSeries(series),
   148	            }))
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    @computed get isFocusModeActive(): boolean {
   152	        return this.props.focusedSeriesName !== undefined
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    @computed private get areas(): React.ReactElement[] {
   156	        const { placedSeriesArr } = this
   157	        const { dualAxis, focusedSeriesName } = this.props
   158	        const { verticalAxis } = dualAxis
   159	
   160	        return placedSeriesArr.map((series, index) => {
   161	            const { placedPoints } = series
   162	            let prevPoints: Array<StackedPlacedPoint>
   163	            if (index > 0) {
   164	                prevPoints = placedSeriesArr[index - 1].placedPoints
   165	            } else {
   166	                prevPoints = [
   167	                    [
   168	                        placedPoints[0][0], // placed x coord of first (= leftmost) point in chart
   169	                        verticalAxis.range[0],
   170	                    ],
   171	                    [
   172	                        lastOfNonEmptyArray(placedPoints)[0], // placed x coord of last (= rightmost) point in chart
   173	                        verticalAxis.range[0],
   174	                    ],
   175	                ]
   176	            }
   177	            const points = [...placedPoints, ...prevPoints.toReversed()]
   178	            const opacity = !this.isFocusModeActive
   179	                ? AREA_OPACITY.default // normal opacity
   180	                : focusedSeriesName === series.seriesName
   181	                  ? AREA_OPACITY.focus // hovered
   182	                  : AREA_OPACITY.mute // non-hovered
   183	
   184	            return (
   185	                <path
   186	                    id={makeIdForHumanConsumption(series.seriesName)}
   187	                    className={makeSafeForCSS(series.seriesName) + "-area"}
   188	                    key={series.seriesName + "-area"}
   189	                    strokeLinecap="round"
   190	                    d={pointsToPath(points)}
   191	                    fill={series.color}
   192	                    fillOpacity={opacity}
   193	                    clipPath={this.props.clipPath}
   194	                    onMouseEnter={(): void => {
   195	                        this.props.onAreaMouseEnter?.(series.seriesName)
   196	                    }}
   197	                    onMouseLeave={(): void => {
   198	                        this.props.onAreaMouseLeave?.()
   199	                    }}
   200	                />
   201	            )
   202	        })
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    @computed private get borders(): React.ReactElement[] {
   206	        const { placedSeriesArr } = this
   207	        const { focusedSeriesName } = this.props
   208	
   209	        return placedSeriesArr.map((placedSeries) => {
   210	            const opacity = !this.isFocusModeActive
   211	                ? BORDER_OPACITY.default // normal opacity
   212	                : focusedSeriesName === placedSeries.seriesName
   213	                  ? BORDER_OPACITY.focus // hovered
   214	                  : BORDER_OPACITY.mute // non-hovered
   215	            const strokeWidth =
   216	                focusedSeriesName === placedSeries.seriesName
   217	                    ? BORDER_WIDTH.focus
   218	                    : BORDER_WIDTH.default
   219	
   220	            return (
   221	                <path
   222	                    id={makeIdForHumanConsumption(placedSeries.seriesName)}
   223	                    className={
   224	                        makeSafeForCSS(placedSeries.seriesName) + "-border"
   225	                    }
   226	                    key={placedSeries.seriesName + "-border"}
   227	                    strokeLinecap="round"
   228	                    d={pointsToPath(placedSeries.placedPoints)}
   229	                    stroke={rgb(placedSeries.color).darker(0.5).toString()}
   230	                    strokeOpacity={opacity}
   231	                    strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
   232	                    fill="none"
   233	                    clipPath={this.props.clipPath}
   234	                    onMouseEnter={(): void => {
   235	                        this.props.onAreaMouseEnter?.(placedSeries.seriesName)
   236	                    }}
   237	                    onMouseLeave={(): void => {
   238	                        this.props.onAreaMouseLeave?.()
   239	                    }}
   240	                />
   241	            )
   242	        })
   243	    }
   244	
   245	    render(): React.ReactElement {
   246	        return (
   247	            <g
   248	                className="Areas"
   249	                id={makeIdForHumanConsumption("stacked-areas")}
   250	            >
   251	                <g id={makeIdForHumanConsumption("areas")}>{this.areas}</g>
   252	                <g id={makeIdForHumanConsumption("borders")}>{this.borders}</g>
   253	            </g>
   254	        )
   255	    }
   256	}

   258	@observer
   259	export class StackedAreaChart extends AbstractStackedChart {

   264	    @computed protected get yAxisDomain(): [number, number] {
   265	        const yValues = this.allStackedPoints.map(
   266	            (point) => point.value + point.valueOffset
   267	        )
   268	        return [0, _.max(yValues) ?? 0]
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    @computed protected get xAxisConfig(): AxisConfig {
   272	        return new AxisConfig(
   273	            {
   274	                hideGridlines: true,
   275	                ...this.manager.xAxisConfig,
   276	            },
   277	            this
   278	        )
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    @computed get midpoints(): number[] {
   282	        let prevY = 0
   283	        return this.series.map((series) => {
   284	            const lastValue = R.last(series.points)
   285	            if (!lastValue) return 0
   286	
   287	            const y = lastValue.value + lastValue.valueOffset
   288	            const middleY = prevY + (y - prevY) / 2
   289	            prevY = y
   290	            return middleY
   291	        })
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    private hoverStateForSeries(
   295	        series: StackedSeries<number>
   296	    ): InteractionState {
   297	        return getHoverStateForSeries(series, {
   298	            isHoverModeActive: this.isHoverModeActive,
   299	            hoveredSeriesNames: this.hoveredSeriesNames,
   300	        })
   301	    }
   302	
   303	    @computed get lineLegendSeries(): LineLabelSeries[] {
   304	        const { midpoints } = this
   305	        return this.series

   307	                color: series.color,
   308	                seriesName: series.seriesName,
   309	                label: series.seriesName,
   310	                yValue: midpoints[index],
   311	                isAllZeros: series.isAllZeros,
   312	                hover: this.hoverStateForSeries(series),
   313	            }))
   314	            .filter((series) => !series.isAllZeros)
   315	            .toReversed()
   316	    }
   317	
   318	    @computed get maxLineLegendWidth(): number {
   319	        return Math.min(150, this.bounds.width / 3)
   320	    }
   321	
   322	    @computed get lineLegendWidth(): number {
   323	        if (!this.manager.showLegend) return 0
   324

   326	        // the width to avoid circular dependencies
   327	        return LineLegend.stableWidth({
   328	            series: this.lineLegendSeries,
   329	            maxWidth: this.maxLineLegendWidth,
   330	            fontSize: this.fontSize,
   331	        })
   332	    }
   333	
   334	    @observable tooltipState = new TooltipState<{
   335	        index: number // time-index into points array
   336	        series?: SeriesName
   337	    }>({ fade: "immediate" })
   338	
   339	    @action.bound private onAreaMouseEnter(seriesName: SeriesName): void {
   340	        if (this.tooltipState.target) {
   341	            _.extend(this.tooltipState.target, { series: seriesName })
   342	        } else {
   343	            this.tooltipState.target = {
   344	                index: 0, // might be incorrect but will be updated immediately by the move event handler
   345	                series: seriesName,
   346	            }
   347	        }
   348	    }
   349	
   350	    @action.bound private onAreaMouseLeave(): void {
   351	        _.extend(this.tooltipState.target, { series: undefined })
   352	    }
   353	
   354	    @observable lineLegendHoveredSeriesName?: SeriesName
   355	    @observable private hoverTimer?: NodeJS.Timeout
   356	
   357	    @computed protected get paddingForLegendRight(): number {
   358	        return this.lineLegendWidth
   359	    }
   360	
   361	    @computed get seriesSortedByImportance(): string[] {
   362	        return this.series
   363	            .toSorted(
   364	                (
   365	                    s1: StackedSeries<number>,
   366	                    s2: StackedSeries<number>
   367	                ): number => {
   368	                    const PREFER_S1 = -1
   369	                    const PREFER_S2 = 1
   370	
   371	                    if (!s1) return PREFER_S2
   372	                    if (!s2) return PREFER_S1
   373	
   374	                    // early return if one series is all zeroes
   375	                    if (s1.isAllZeros && !s2.isAllZeros) return PREFER_S2
   376	                    if (s2.isAllZeros && !s1.isAllZeros) return PREFER_S1
   377	
   378	                    // prefer series with a higher maximum value
   379	                    const yMax1 = _.maxBy(s1.points, (p) => p.value)?.value ?? 0
   380	                    const yMax2 = _.maxBy(s2.points, (p) => p.value)?.value ?? 0
   381	                    if (yMax1 > yMax2) return PREFER_S1
   382	                    if (yMax2 > yMax1) return PREFER_S2
   383	
   384	                    // prefer series with a higher last value
   385	                    const yLast1 = R.last(s1.points)?.value ?? 0
   386	                    const yLast2 = R.last(s2.points)?.value ?? 0
   387	                    if (yLast1 > yLast2) return PREFER_S1
   388	                    if (yLast2 > yLast1) return PREFER_S2
   389	
   390	                    // prefer series with a higher total area
   391	                    const area1 = _.sumBy(s1.points, (p) => p.value)
   392	                    const area2 = _.sumBy(s2.points, (p) => p.value)
   393	                    if (area1 > area2) return PREFER_S1
   394	                    if (area2 > area1) return PREFER_S2
   395	
   396	                    return 0
   397	                }
   398	            )
   399	            .map((s) => s.seriesName)
   400	    }
   401	
   402	    @action.bound onLineLegendMouseOver(seriesName: SeriesName): void {
   403	        clearTimeout(this.hoverTimer)
   404	        this.lineLegendHoveredSeriesName = seriesName
   405	    }
   406	
   407	    @action.bound onLineLegendMouseLeave(): void {
   408	        clearTimeout(this.hoverTimer)
   409	        this.hoverTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   410	            // wait before clearing selection in case the mouse is moving quickly over neighboring labels
   411	            this.lineLegendHoveredSeriesName = undefined
   412	        }, 200)
   413	    }
   414	
   415	    @computed get facetLegendHoveredSeriesName(): SeriesName | undefined {
   416	        const { externalLegendHoverBin } = this.manager
   417	        if (!externalLegendHoverBin) return undefined
   418	        // stacked area charts can't plot the same entity or column multiple times,
   419	        // so we just find the first series that matches the hovered legend item
   420	        const hoveredSeries = this.rawSeries.find((series) =>
   421	            externalLegendHoverBin.contains(series.seriesName)
   422	        )
   423	        return hoveredSeries?.seriesName
   424	    }
   425	
   426	    @computed get hoveredSeriesName(): SeriesName | undefined {
   427	        return (
   428	            // if the chart area is hovered
   429	            this.tooltipState.target?.series ??
   430	            // if the line legend is hovered
   431	            this.lineLegendHoveredSeriesName ?? // if the facet legend is hovered
   432	            this.facetLegendHoveredSeriesName
   433	        )
   434	    }
   435

   439	            // if the external legend is hovered, we want to mute
   440	            // all non-hovered series even if the chart doesn't plot
   441	            // the currently hovered series
   442	            !!this.manager.externalLegendHoverBin
   443	        )
   444	    }

   447	        return this.hoveredSeriesName ? [this.hoveredSeriesName] : []

     5	    findGreatestCommonDivisorOfArray,
     6	    rollingMap,

     9	import { StackedPointPositionType, StackedSeries } from "./StackedConstants"
    10	
    11	// This method shift up the Y Values of a Series with Points in place.
    12	export const stackSeries = <PositionType extends StackedPointPositionType>(
    13	    seriesArr: readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[]
    14	): readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[] => {
    15	    seriesArr.forEach((series, seriesIndex) => {
    16	        if (!seriesIndex) return // The first series does not need to be shifted
    17	        series.points.forEach((point, pointIndex) => {
    18	            const pointBelowThisOne =
    19	                seriesArr[seriesIndex - 1].points[pointIndex]
    20	            point.valueOffset =
    21	                pointBelowThisOne.value + pointBelowThisOne.valueOffset
    22	        })
    23	    })
    24	    return seriesArr
    25	}
    26	
    27	// This method shifts up positive y values and shifts down negative y values of a Series with Points in place.
    28	export const stackSeriesInBothDirections = <
    29	    PositionType extends StackedPointPositionType,
    30	>(
    31	    seriesArr: readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[]
    32	): readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[] => {
    33	    seriesArr.forEach((series, seriesIndex) => {
    34	        if (!seriesIndex) return // The first series does not need to be shifted
    35	        series.points.forEach((point, pointIndex) => {
    36	            const pointsBelowThisOne = seriesArr
    37	                .slice(0, seriesIndex)
    38	                .map((s) => s.points[pointIndex])
    39	            const pointBelowThisOne =
    40	                point.value < 0
    41	                    ? pointsBelowThisOne.findLast((p) => p.value < 0)
    42	                    : pointsBelowThisOne.findLast((p) => p.value >= 0)
    43	            point.valueOffset = pointBelowThisOne
    44	                ? pointBelowThisOne.value + pointBelowThisOne.valueOffset
    45	                : 0
    46	        })
    47	    })
    48	    return seriesArr
    49	}
    50	
    51	// Makes sure that values are evenly spaced
    52	export function withUniformSpacing(values: number[]): number[] {
    53	    const deltas = rollingMap(values, (a, b) => b - a)
    54	    const gcd = findGreatestCommonDivisorOfArray(deltas)
    55	    if (gcd === null) return values
    56	    return _.range(values[0], values[values.length - 1] + gcd, gcd)
    57	}
    58	
    59	// Adds a Y = 0 value for each missing x value (where X is usually Time)
    60	export const withMissingValuesAsZeroes = <
    61	    PositionType extends StackedPointPositionType,
    62	>(
    63	    seriesArr: readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[],
    64	    { enforceUniformSpacing = false }: { enforceUniformSpacing?: boolean } = {}
    65	): StackedSeries<PositionType>[] => {
    66	    let allXValuesSorted = sortNumeric(
    67	        _.uniq(
    68	            seriesArr
    69	                .flatMap((series) => series.points)
    70	                .map((point) => point.position)
    71	        )
    72	    )
    73	
    74	    if (enforceUniformSpacing && isArrayOfNumbers(allXValuesSorted)) {
    75	        allXValuesSorted = withUniformSpacing(
    76	            allXValuesSorted
    77	        ) as PositionType[]
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    return seriesArr.map((series) => {
    81	        const pointsByPosition = _.keyBy(series.points, "position")
    82	        return {
    83	            ...series,
    84	            points: allXValuesSorted.map((position) => {
    85	                const point = pointsByPosition[position]
    86	                const value = point?.value ?? 0
    87	                const time = point?.time ?? 0
    88	                return omitUndefinedValues({
    89	                    time,
    90	                    position,
    91	                    value,
    92	                    valueOffset: 0,
    93	                    interpolated: point?.interpolated,
    94	                    fake: !point || !!point.interpolated,
    95	                    color: point?.color,
    96	                })
    97	            }),
    98	        }
    99	    })
   100	}

   162	it("should mark interpolated values as fake", () => {
   163	    const csv = `gdp,year,entityName
   164	    10,2000,france
   165	    0,2001,france
   166	    ,2002,france
   167	    ,2003,france
   168	    8,2005,france
   169	    ,2006,france
   170	    2,2000,uk
   171	    3,2004,uk`
   172	    const table = new OwidTable(csv, [
   173	        { slug: "gdp", type: ColumnTypeNames.Numeric },
   174	        { slug: "year", type: ColumnTypeNames.Year },
   175	    ])
   176	
   177	    const manager: ChartManager = {
   178	        table,
   179	        yColumnSlugs: ["gdp"],
   180	        selection: table.availableEntityNames,
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    const chart = new StackedAreaChart({ manager })
   184	
   185	    // indices are reversed because stacked charts reverse the stacking order
   186	    const pointsFrance = chart.series[1].points
   187	    const pointsUK = chart.series[0].points
   188	
   189	    // year 2000
   190	    expect(pointsFrance[0].interpolated).toBeFalsy()
   191	    expect(pointsFrance[0].fake).toBeFalsy()
   192	    expect(pointsUK[0].interpolated).toBeFalsy()
   193	    expect(pointsUK[0].fake).toBeFalsy()
   194	
   195	    // year = 2001
   196	    expect(pointsFrance[1].interpolated).toBeFalsy()
   197	    expect(pointsFrance[1].fake).toBeFalsy()
   198	    expect(pointsUK[1].interpolated).toBeTruthy()
   199	    expect(pointsUK[1].fake).toBeTruthy()
   200	
   201	    // year = 2004
   202	    expect(pointsFrance[2].interpolated).toBeTruthy()
   203	    expect(pointsFrance[2].fake).toBeTruthy()
   204	    expect(pointsUK[2].interpolated).toBeFalsy()
   205	    expect(pointsUK[2].fake).toBeFalsy()
   206	
   207	    // year = 2005
   208	    expect(pointsFrance[3].interpolated).toBeFalsy()
   209	    expect(pointsFrance[3].fake).toBeFalsy()
   210	    expect(pointsUK[3].interpolated).toBeFalsy()
   211	    expect(pointsUK[3].fake).toBeTruthy() // true since it's zero-filled
   212	})

    53	
    54	// used in StackedBar charts to color negative and positive bars
    55	const POSITIVE_COLOR = BinaryMapPaletteE.colorSets[0][0] // orange
    56	const NEGATIVE_COLOR = BinaryMapPaletteE.colorSets[0][1] // blue
    57	
    58	export interface AbstractStackedChartProps {
    59	    bounds?: Bounds
    60	    manager: ChartManager
    61	    enableLinearInterpolation?: boolean // defaults to true
    62	}
    63	
    64	@observer
    65	export class AbstractStackedChart
    66	    extends React.Component<AbstractStackedChartProps>
    67	    implements ChartInterface, AxisManager
    68	{
    69	    transformTable(table: OwidTable): OwidTable {
    70	        table = table.filterByEntityNames(
    71	            this.selectionArray.selectedEntityNames
    72	        )
    73	
    74	        // TODO: remove this filter once we don't have mixed type columns in datasets
    75	        table = table
    76	            .replaceNonNumericCellsWithErrorValues(this.yColumnSlugs)
    77	            .dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAllColumns(this.yColumnSlugs)
    78	
    79	        if (this.shouldRunLinearInterpolation) {
    80	            this.yColumnSlugs.forEach((slug) => {
    81	                table = table.interpolateColumnLinearly(slug)
    82	            })
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        // Drop rows for which no valid data points exist for any display column
    86	        // after interpolation, which most likely means they lie at the start/end
    87	        // of the time range and were not extrapolated
    88	        if (this.missingDataStrategy !== MissingDataStrategy.show) {
    89	            table = table.dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAnyColumn(this.yColumnSlugs)
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        if (this.manager.isRelativeMode) {
    93	            table = this.isEntitySeries
    94	                ? table.toPercentageFromEachEntityForEachTime(
    95	                      this.yColumnSlugs[0]
    96	                  )
    97	                : table.toPercentageFromEachColumnForEachEntityAndTime(
    98	                      this.yColumnSlugs
    99	                  )
   100	        }
   101	        return table
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    transformTableForSelection(table: OwidTable): OwidTable {
   105	        // if entities with partial data are not plotted,
   106	        // make sure they don't show up in the entity selector
   107	        if (this.missingDataStrategy !== MissingDataStrategy.show) {
   108	            table = table
   109	                .replaceNonNumericCellsWithErrorValues(this.yColumnSlugs)
   110	                .dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAllColumns(this.yColumnSlugs)
   111	
   112	            if (this.shouldRunLinearInterpolation) {
   113	                this.yColumnSlugs.forEach((slug) => {
   114	                    table = table.interpolateColumnLinearly(slug)
   115	                })
   116	            }
   117	
   118	            table = table.dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAnyColumn(this.yColumnSlugs)
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        return table
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    @computed private get missingDataStrategy(): MissingDataStrategy {
   125	        return this.manager.missingDataStrategy || MissingDataStrategy.auto
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    @computed get shouldRunLinearInterpolation(): boolean {
   129	        // enabled by default
   130	        return this.props.enableLinearInterpolation ?? true
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    @computed get inputTable(): OwidTable {
   134	        return this.manager.table
   135	    }
   136	
   137	    @computed get transformedTable(): OwidTable {
   138	        return (
   139	            this.manager.transformedTable ??
   140	            this.transformTable(this.inputTable)
   141	        )
   142	    }
   143	
   144	    @computed get manager(): ChartManager {
   145	        return this.props.manager
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    @computed get bounds(): Bounds {
   149	        return this.props.bounds ?? DEFAULT_BOUNDS
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    @computed get isStatic(): boolean {
   153	        return this.manager.isStatic ?? false
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    @computed get fontSize(): number {
   157	        return this.manager.fontSize ?? BASE_FONT_SIZE
   158	    }
   159	
   160	    @computed get detailsOrderedByReference(): string[] {
   161	        return this.manager.detailsOrderedByReference ?? []
   162	    }
   163	
   164	    protected get paddingForLegendRight(): number {
   165	        return 0
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    protected get paddingForLegendTop(): number {
   169	        return 0
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    @computed get renderUid(): number {
   173	        return guid()
   174	    }
   175	
   176	    @computed protected get yColumns(): CoreColumn[] {
   177	        return this.transformedTable.getColumns(this.yColumnSlugs)
   178	    }
   179

   213	    @computed get seriesStrategy(): SeriesStrategy {

   273	    @computed protected get yAxisDomain(): [number, number] {
   274	        return [0, 0]
   275	    }
   276	
   277	    @computed private get verticalAxisPart(): VerticalAxis {
   278	        const axis = this.yAxisConfig.toVerticalAxis()
   279	        // Use user settings for axis, unless relative mode
   280	        if (this.manager.isRelativeMode) axis.domain = [0, 100]
   281	        else axis.updateDomainPreservingUserSettings(this.yAxisDomain)
   282	        axis.formatColumn = this.yColumns[0]
   283	        return axis
   284	    }
   285	
   286	    @computed
   287	    private get columnsAsSeries(): readonly StackedRawSeries<number>[] {
   288	        return this.yColumns
   289	            .map((col) => {
   290	                return {
   291	                    isProjection: col.isProjection,
   292	                    seriesName: col.displayName,
   293	                    rows: col.owidRows,
   294	                }
   295	            })
   296	            .toReversed() // For stacked charts, we want the first selected series to be on top, so we reverse the order of the stacks.
   297	    }
   298	
   299	    @computed
   300	    private get entitiesAsSeries(): readonly StackedRawSeries<number>[] {
   301	        if (!this.yColumns.length) return []
   302	
   303	        const { isProjection, owidRowsByEntityName } = this.yColumns[0]
   304	        return this.selectionArray.selectedEntityNames
   305	            .map((seriesName) => {
   306	                return {
   307	                    isProjection,
   308	                    seriesName,
   309	                    rows: owidRowsByEntityName.get(seriesName) || [],
   310	                }
   311	            })
   312	            .toReversed() // For stacked charts, we want the first selected series to be on top, so we reverse the order of the stacks.
   313	    }
   314	
   315	    @computed
   316	    protected get rawSeries(): readonly StackedRawSeries<number>[] {
   317	        return this.isEntitySeries
   318	            ? this.entitiesAsSeries
   319	            : this.columnsAsSeries
   320	    }
   321	
   322	    @computed
   323	    protected get allStackedPoints(): readonly StackedPoint<number>[] {
   324	        return this.series.flatMap((series) => series.points)
   325	    }
   326	
   327	    @computed get failMessage(): string {
   328	        const { yColumnSlugs } = this
   329	        if (!yColumnSlugs.length) return "Missing variable"
   330	        if (!this.series.length) return "No matching data"
   331	        if (!this.allStackedPoints.length) return "No matching points"
   332	        return ""
   333	    }

   335	    @computed private get colorMap(): CategoricalColorMap {

   338	            : this.inputTable.columnDisplayNameToColorMap
   339	    }
   340	
   341	    @computed private get categoricalColorAssigner(): CategoricalColorAssigner {
   342	        const seriesCount = this.isEntitySeries
   343	            ? this.selectionArray.numSelectedEntities
   344	            : this.yColumns.length
   345	        return new CategoricalColorAssigner({
   346	            colorScheme:
   347	                (this.manager.baseColorScheme
   348	                    ? ColorSchemes.get(this.manager.baseColorScheme)
   349	                    : null) ??
   350	                ColorSchemes.get(ColorSchemeName.stackedAreaDefault),
   351	            invertColorScheme: this.manager.invertColorScheme,
   352	            colorMap: this.colorMap,
   353	            autoColorMapCache: this.manager.seriesColorMap,
   354	            numColorsInUse: seriesCount,
   355	        })
   356	    }
   357	
   358	    @computed protected get selectionArray(): SelectionArray {
   359	        return makeSelectionArray(this.manager.selection)
   360	    }
   361	
   362	    @computed get isEntitySeries(): boolean {
   363	        return this.seriesStrategy === SeriesStrategy.entity
   364	    }
   365	
   366	    @computed get seriesColors(): string[] {
   367	        return this.series.map((series) => series.color)
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    @computed get availableFacetStrategies(): FacetStrategy[] {
   371	        const strategies: FacetStrategy[] = []
   372	
   373	        const { selectedEntityNames } = this.selectionArray
   374	        const areMultipleEntitiesSelected = selectedEntityNames.length > 1
   375	        const hasMultipleYColumns = this.yColumns.length > 1
   376	        const shortUnits = this.yColumns.map((column) => column.shortUnit)
   377	        const uniqueUnits = new Set(shortUnits)
   378	        const hasMultipleUnits = uniqueUnits.size > 1
   379	        const hasPercentageUnit = shortUnits.some(
   380	            (shortUnit) => shortUnit === "%"
   381	        )
   382	
   383	        // Normally StackedArea/StackedBar charts are always single-entity or single-column,
   384	        // but if we are ever in a mode where we have multiple entities selected (e.g. through
   385	        // GlobalEntitySelector) and multiple columns, it only makes sense when faceted.
   386	        if (
   387	            // No facet strategy makes sense if columns are stacked and a single entity is selected
   388	            (!this.isEntitySeries && !areMultipleEntitiesSelected) ||
   389	            // No facet strategy makes sense if entities are stacked and we have a single column
   390	            (this.isEntitySeries &&
   391	                !hasMultipleYColumns &&
   392	                // The stacking must be sensible
   393	                checkIsStackingEntitiesSensible(selectedEntityNames))
   394	        )
   395	            strategies.push(FacetStrategy.none)
   396	
   397	        if (
   398	            // Facetting by entity makes sense if multiple entities are selected
   399	            areMultipleEntitiesSelected &&
   400	            // Stacking columns with different units isn't allowed
   401	            !hasMultipleUnits
   402	        )
   403	            strategies.push(FacetStrategy.entity)
   404	
   405	        if (
   406	            // Facetting by column makes sense if we have multiple columns
   407	            hasMultipleYColumns &&
   408	            // Stacking percentages doesn't make sense unless we're in relative mode
   409	            (!hasPercentageUnit || this.manager.isRelativeMode) &&
   410	            // Some stacked entity combinations are not allowed, e.g. stacking
   411	            // countries on top their continent or stacking countries or continents
   412	            // on top of World
   413	            checkIsStackingEntitiesSensible(selectedEntityNames)
   414	        )
   415	            strategies.push(FacetStrategy.metric)
   416	
   417	        return strategies
   418	    }
   419	
   420	    @computed get shouldUseValueBasedColorScheme(): boolean {
   421	        return false
   422	    }
   423	
   424	    @computed get useValueBasedColorScheme(): boolean {
   425	        return false
   426	    }
   427	
   428	    @computed get unstackedSeries(): readonly StackedSeries<number>[] {
   429	        return this.rawSeries
   430	            .filter((series) => series.rows.length > 0)
   431	
   432	            .map((series) => {
   433	                const { isProjection, seriesName, rows } = series
   434	
   435	                const points = rows.map((row) => {
   436	                    const pointColor =
   437	                        row.value > 0 ? POSITIVE_COLOR : NEGATIVE_COLOR
   438	                    return {
   439	                        position: row.originalTime,
   440	                        time: row.originalTime,
   441	                        value: row.value,
   442	                        valueOffset: 0,
   443	                        interpolated:
   444	                            this.shouldRunLinearInterpolation &&
   445	                            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(row.value) &&
   446	                            !isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(row.originalValue),
   447	                        // takes precedence over the series color if given
   448	                        color: this.useValueBasedColorScheme
   449	                            ? pointColor
   450	                            : undefined,
   451	                    }
   452	                })
   453	
   454	                return {
   455	                    seriesName,
   456	                    isProjection,
   457	                    points,
   458	                    isAllZeros: points.every((point) => point.value === 0),
   459	                    color: this.categoricalColorAssigner.assign(seriesName),
   460	                }
   461	            }) as StackedSeries<number>[]
   462	    }

    19	enum TransformParamType {
    20	    TimeSlug = "TimeSlug", // column with time
    21	    EntitySlug = "EntitySlug", // column with entity

    38	// In Grapher we return just the years for which we have values for. This puts MissingValuePlaceholder
    39	// in the spots where we are missing values (added to make computing rolling windows easier).
    40	// Takes an array of value/year pairs and expands it so that there is an undefined
    41	// for each missing value from the first year to the last year, preserving the position of
    42	// the existing values.
    43	export const insertMissingValuePlaceholders = (
    44	    values: number[],
    45	    times: number[]
    46	): (number | MissingValuePlaceholder)[] => {
    47	    const startTime = times[0]
    48	    const endTime = times[times.length - 1]
    49	    const filledRange = []
    50	    let time = startTime
    51	    const timeToValueIndex = new Map()
    52	    times.forEach((time, index) => {
    53	        timeToValueIndex.set(time, index)
    54	    })
    55	    while (time <= endTime) {
    56	        filledRange.push(
    57	            timeToValueIndex.has(time)
    58	                ? values[timeToValueIndex.get(time)]
    59	                : ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder
    60	        )
    61	        time++
    62	    }
    63	    return filledRange
    64	}
    65	
    66	// todo: add the precision param to ensure no floating point effects
    67	export function computeRollingAverage(
    68	    numbers: (number | undefined | null | ErrorValue)[],
    69	    windowSize: number,
    70	    align: "right" | "center" = "right"
    71	): (number | ErrorValue)[] {
    72	    const result: (number | ErrorValue)[] = []
    73	
    74	    for (let valueIndex = 0; valueIndex < numbers.length; valueIndex++) {
    75	        // If a value is undefined in the original input, keep it undefined in the output
    76	        const currentVal = numbers[valueIndex]
    77	        if (currentVal === null) {
    78	            result[valueIndex] = ErrorValueTypes.NullButShouldBeNumber
    79	            continue
    80	        } else if (currentVal === undefined) {
    81	            result[valueIndex] = ErrorValueTypes.UndefinedButShouldBeNumber
    82	            continue
    83	        } else if (currentVal instanceof ErrorValue) {
    84	            result[valueIndex] = currentVal
    85	            continue
    86	        }
    87	
    88	        // Take away 1 for the current value (windowSize=1 means no smoothing & no expansion)
    89	        const expand = windowSize - 1
    90	
    91	        // With centered smoothing, expand uneven windows asymmetrically (ceil & floor) to ensure
    92	        // a correct number of window values get taken into account.
    93	        // Arbitrarily biased towards left (past).
    94	        const expandLeft = align === "center" ? Math.ceil(expand / 2) : expand
    95	        const expandRight = align === "center" ? Math.floor(expand / 2) : 0
    96	
    97	        const startIndex = Math.max(valueIndex - expandLeft, 0)
    98	        const endIndex = Math.min(valueIndex + expandRight, numbers.length - 1)
    99	
   100	        let count = 0
   101	        let sum = 0
   102	        for (
   103	            let windowIndex = startIndex;
   104	            windowIndex <= endIndex;
   105	            windowIndex++
   106	        ) {
   107	            const value = numbers[windowIndex]
   108	            if (
   109	                value !== undefined &&
   110	                value !== null &&
   111	                !(value instanceof ErrorValue)
   112	            ) {
   113	                sum += value!
   114	                count++
   115	            }
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        result[valueIndex] = sum / count
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    return result
   122	}

   124	// Assumptions: data is sorted by entity, then time
   125	// todo: move tests over from CE
   126	const timeSinceEntityExceededThreshold: Transform = {
   127	    params: [
   128	        { type: TransformParamType.TimeSlug },
   129	        { type: TransformParamType.EntitySlug },
   130	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   131	        { type: TransformParamType.String },
   132	    ],
   133	    fn: (
   134	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   135	        timeSlug: ColumnSlug,
   136	        entitySlug: ColumnSlug,
   137	        columnSlug: ColumnSlug,
   138	        thresholdAsString: string
   139	    ): (number | ValueTooLow)[] => {
   140	        const threshold = parseFloat(thresholdAsString)
   141	        const groupValues = columnStore[entitySlug] as string[]
   142	        const columnValues = columnStore[columnSlug] as number[]
   143	        const timeValues = columnStore[timeSlug] as number[]
   144	        let currentGroup: string
   145	        let groupExceededThresholdAtTime: number
   146	        return columnValues.map((value, index) => {
   147	            const group = groupValues[index]
   148	            const currentTime = timeValues[index]
   149	            if (group !== currentGroup) {
   150	                if (!isNotErrorValue(value)) return value
   151	                if (value < threshold) return ErrorValueTypes.ValueTooLow
   152	
   153	                currentGroup = group
   154	                groupExceededThresholdAtTime = currentTime
   155	            }
   156	            return currentTime - groupExceededThresholdAtTime
   157	        })
   158	    },
   159	}
   160	
   161	// Assumptions: data is sorted by entity, then time
   162	// todo: move tests over from CE
   163	const rollingAverage: Transform = {
   164	    params: [
   165	        { type: TransformParamType.TimeSlug },
   166	        { type: TransformParamType.EntitySlug },
   167	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   168	        { type: TransformParamType.Number },
   169	    ],
   170	    fn: (
   171	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   172	        timeSlug: ColumnSlug,
   173	        entitySlug: ColumnSlug,
   174	        columnSlug: ColumnSlug,
   175	        windowSize: number
   176	    ): (number | ErrorValue)[] => {
   177	        const entityNames = columnStore[entitySlug] as string[]
   178	        const columnValues = columnStore[columnSlug] as number[]
   179	        const timeValues = columnStore[timeSlug] as number[]
   180	        const len = entityNames.length
   181	        if (!len) return []
   182	        let currentEntity = entityNames[0]
   183	        let currentValues: number[] = []
   184	        let currentTimes: Time[] = []
   185	
   186	        const groups: (number | ErrorValue)[][] = []
   187	        for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex <= len; rowIndex++) {
   188	            const entityName = entityNames[rowIndex]
   189	            const value = columnValues[rowIndex]
   190	            const time = timeValues[rowIndex]
   191	            if (currentEntity !== entityName) {
   192	                const averages = computeRollingAverage(
   193	                    insertMissingValuePlaceholders(currentValues, currentTimes),
   194	                    windowSize
   195	                ).filter(
   196	                    (value) =>
   197	                        !(value === ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder)
   198	                ) // filter the placeholders back out
   199	                groups.push(averages)
   200	                if (value === undefined) break // We iterate to <= so that we push the last row
   201	                currentValues = []
   202	                currentTimes = []
   203	                currentEntity = entityName
   204	            }
   205	            currentValues.push(value)
   206	            currentTimes.push(time)
   207	        }
   208	        return groups.flat()
   209	    },
   210	}

   212	const divideBy: Transform = {
   213	    params: [
   214	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   215	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   216	    ],
   217	    fn: (
   218	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   219	        numeratorSlug: ColumnSlug,
   220	        denominatorSlug: ColumnSlug
   221	    ): (number | DivideByZeroError)[] => {
   222	        const numeratorValues = columnStore[numeratorSlug] as number[]
   223	        const denominatorValues = columnStore[denominatorSlug] as number[]
   224	        return denominatorValues.map((denominator, index) => {
   225	            if (denominator === 0) return ErrorValueTypes.DivideByZeroError
   226	            const numerator = numeratorValues[index]
   227	            if (!isNotErrorValue(numerator)) return numerator
   228	            if (!isNotErrorValue(denominator)) return denominator
   229	            return numerator / denominator
   230	        })
   231	    },
   232	}
   233	
   234	const multiplyBy: Transform = {
   235	    params: [
   236	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   237	        { type: TransformParamType.Number },
   238	    ],
   239	    fn: (
   240	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   241	        columnSlug: ColumnSlug,
   242	        factor: number
   243	    ): (number | ErrorValue)[] =>
   244	        columnStore[columnSlug].map((value) =>
   245	            isNotErrorValue(value) ? (value as number) * factor : value
   246	        ),
   247	}

   249	const subtract: Transform = {
   250	    params: [
   251	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   252	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   253	    ],
   254	    fn: (
   255	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   256	        columnSlugA: ColumnSlug,
   257	        columnSlugB: ColumnSlug
   258	    ): number[] => {
   259	        const values = columnStore[columnSlugA] as number[]
   260	        const subValues = columnStore[columnSlugB] as number[]
   261	        return subValues.map((subValue, index) => {
   262	            const value = values[index]
   263	            if (!isNotErrorValue(value)) return value
   264	            if (!isNotErrorValue(subValue)) return subValue
   265	            return value - subValue
   266	        })
   267	    },
   268	}

   270	enum WhereOperators {
   271	    is = "is",
   272	    isNot = "isNot",
   273	    isGreaterThan = "isGreaterThan",
   274	    isGreaterThanOrEqual = "isGreaterThanOrEqual",
   275	    isLessThan = "isLessThan",
   276	    isLessThanOrEqual = "isLessThanOrEqual",
   277	}
   278	// Todo: add tests/expand capabilities/remove?
   279	// Currently this just supports `columnSlug where someColumnSlug (isNot|is) this or that or this`
   280	const where: Transform = {
   281	    params: [
   282	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   283	        {
   284	            type: TransformParamType.ColumnSlug,
   285	        },
   286	        {
   287	            type: TransformParamType.String,
   288	            spread: true,
   289	        },
   290	    ],
   291	    fn: (
   292	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   293	        columnSlug: ColumnSlug,
   294	        conditionSlug: ColumnSlug,
   295	        ...condition: string[]
   296	    ): CoreValueType[] => {
   297	        const values = columnStore[columnSlug]
   298	        const conditionValues = columnStore[conditionSlug]
   299	        const operator = condition.shift()
   300	        let passes: (value: any) => boolean = () => true
   301	        if (
   302	            operator === WhereOperators.isNot ||
   303	            operator === WhereOperators.is
   304	        ) {
   305	            const result = operator === "isNot" ? false : true
   306	            const list = condition.join(" ").split(" or ")
   307	            const set = new Set(list)
   308	            passes = (value: any): boolean =>
   309	                set.has(value) ? result : !result
   310	        } else if (operator === WhereOperators.isGreaterThan)
   311	            passes = (value: any): boolean =>
   312	                value > parseFloat(condition.join(""))
   313	        else if (operator === WhereOperators.isGreaterThanOrEqual)
   314	            passes = (value: any): boolean =>
   315	                value >= parseFloat(condition.join(""))
   316	        else if (operator === WhereOperators.isLessThan)
   317	            passes = (value: any): boolean =>
   318	                value < parseFloat(condition.join(""))
   319	        else if (operator === WhereOperators.isLessThanOrEqual)
   320	            passes = (value: any): boolean =>
   321	                value <= parseFloat(condition.join(""))
   322	
   323	        return values.map((value, index) =>
   324	            passes(conditionValues[index])
   325	                ? value
   326	                : ErrorValueTypes.FilteredValue
   327	        )
   328	    },
   329	}
   330	
   331	// Assumptions: data is sorted by entity, then time, and time is a continous integer with a row for each time step.
   332	// todo: move tests over from CE
   333	const percentChange: Transform = {
   334	    params: [
   335	        { type: TransformParamType.TimeSlug },
   336	        { type: TransformParamType.EntitySlug },
   337	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   338	        { type: TransformParamType.Number },
   339	    ],
   340	    fn: (
   341	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   342	        timeSlug: ColumnSlug,
   343	        entitySlug: ColumnSlug,
   344	        columnSlug: ColumnSlug,
   345	        windowSize: number
   346	    ): (number | ErrorValue)[] => {
   347	        const entityNames = columnStore[entitySlug] as string[]
   348	        const columnValues = columnStore[columnSlug] as number[]
   349	
   350	        // If windowSize is 0 then there is zero change for every valid value
   351	        if (!windowSize)
   352	            return columnValues.map((val) => (isNotErrorValue(val) ? 0 : val))
   353	
   354	        let currentEntity: string
   355	        return columnValues.map((value: any, index) => {
   356	            const entity = entityNames[index]
   357	            const previousEntity = entityNames[index - windowSize] as any
   358	            const previousValue = columnValues[index - windowSize] as any
   359	            if (
   360	                !currentEntity ||
   361	                currentEntity !== entity ||
   362	                previousEntity !== entity
   363	            ) {
   364	                currentEntity = entity
   365	                return ErrorValueTypes.NoValueToCompareAgainst
   366	            }
   367	            if (previousValue instanceof ErrorValue) return previousValue
   368	            if (value instanceof ErrorValue) return value
   369	
   370	            if (previousValue === 0) return ErrorValueTypes.DivideByZeroError
   371	            if (previousValue === undefined)
   372	                return ErrorValueTypes.NoValueToCompareAgainst
   373	
   374	            return (100 * (value - previousValue)) / previousValue
   375	        })
   376	    },
   377	}
   378	
   379	// Todo: remove?
   380	const asPercentageOf: Transform = {
   381	    params: [
   382	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   383	        { type: TransformParamType.DataSlug },
   384	    ],
   385	    fn: (
   386	        columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   387	        numeratorSlug: ColumnSlug,
   388	        denominatorSlug: ColumnSlug
   389	    ): (number | DivideByZeroError)[] =>
   390	        divideBy
   391	            .fn(columnStore, numeratorSlug, denominatorSlug)
   392	            .map((num: any) => (typeof num === "number" ? 100 * num : num)),
   393	}

   403	const availableTransforms: Record<string, Transform> = {
   404	    asPercentageOf,
   405	    timeSinceEntityExceededThreshold,
   406	    divideBy,
   407	    rollingAverage,
   408	    percentChange,
   409	    multiplyBy,

   411	    where,
   412	    duplicate,
   413	} as const

   415	export const AvailableTransforms = Object.keys(availableTransforms)
   416	
   417	export const extractTransformNameAndParams = (
   418	    transform: string
   419	): { transformName: string; params: string[] } | undefined => {
   420	    const words = transform.split(" ")
   421	    const transformName = words.find(
   422	        (word) => availableTransforms[word] !== undefined
   423	    )
   424	    if (!transformName) {
   425	        console.warn(`Warning: transform '${transformName}' not found`)
   426	        return
   427	    }
   428	    const params = words.filter((word) => word !== transformName)
   429	    return { transformName, params }
   430	}
   431	
   432	export const applyTransforms = (
   433	    columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   434	    defs: CoreColumnDef[]
   435	): CoreColumnStore => {
   436	    for (const def of defs) {
   437	        if (!def.transform || def.transformHasRun) continue
   438	        const { transformName, params = [] } =
   439	            extractTransformNameAndParams(def.transform!) ?? {}
   440	        if (!transformName) continue
   441	        const { fn } = availableTransforms[transformName]
   442	        try {
   443	            columnStore[def.slug] = fn(columnStore, ...params)
   444	            def.transformHasRun = true
   445	        } catch (err) {
   446	            console.error(
   447	                `Error performing transform '${def.transform}' for column '${
   448	                    def.slug
   449	                }'. Expected args: ${fn.length}. Provided args: ${
   450	                    1 + params.length
   451	                }. Ran as ${transformName}(columnStore, ${params
   452	                    .map((param) => `"${param}"`)
   453	                    .join(",")}).`
   454	            )
   455	            console.error(err)
   456	        }
   457	    }
   458	    return columnStore
   459	}

   880	    interpolateColumnLinearly(
   881	        columnSlug: ColumnSlug,
   882	        extrapolate: boolean = false
   883	    ): this {
   884	        // If the column doesn't exist, return the table unchanged.
   885	        if (!this.has(columnSlug)) return this
   886	
   887	        const column = this.get(columnSlug)
   888	        const columnDef = column?.def as OwidColumnDef
   889	
   890	        const maybeTimeColumnSlug =
   891	            getOriginalTimeColumnSlug(this, columnSlug) ??
   892	            timeColumnSlugFromColumnDef(columnDef)
   893	        const timeColumn =
   894	            this.get(maybeTimeColumnSlug) ??
   895	            (this.get(OwidTableSlugs.time) as CoreColumn) // CovidTable does not have a day or year column so we need to use time.
   896	
   897	        const originalColumnSlug =
   898	            makeOriginalValueSlugFromColumnSlug(columnSlug)
   899	        const originalColumnDef = {
   900	            ...columnDef,
   901	            slug: originalColumnSlug,
   902	            display: { includeInTable: false },
   903	        }
   904	
   905	        // todo: we can probably do this once early in the pipeline so we dont have to do it again since complete and sort can be expensive.
   906	        const withAllRows = this.complete([
   907	            this.entityNameSlug,
   908	            timeColumn.slug,
   909	        ]).sortBy([this.entityNameSlug, timeColumn.slug])
   910	
   911	        const interpolationResult = this.interpolate(
   912	            withAllRows,
   913	            columnSlug,
   914	            timeColumn.slug,
   915	            linearInterpolation,
   916	            { extrapolateAtStart: extrapolate, extrapolateAtEnd: extrapolate }
   917	        )
   918	
   919	        const columnStore = {
   920	            ...withAllRows.columnStore,
   921	            [originalColumnSlug]: withAllRows.columnStore[columnSlug],
   922	            [columnSlug]: interpolationResult.values,
   923	        }
   924	
   925	        return this.transform(
   926	            columnStore,
   927	            [
   928	                ...this.defs,
   929	                originalColumnDef,
   930	                {
   931	                    ...timeColumn.def,
   932	                },
   933	            ],
   934	            `Interpolated values in column ${columnSlug} linearly and appended column ${originalColumnSlug} with the original values`,
   935	            TransformType.UpdateColumnDefs
   936	        )
   937	    }
   938	
   939	    interpolateColumnsByClosestTimeMatch(
   940	        columnSlugA: ColumnSlug,
   941	        columnSlugB: ColumnSlug
   942	    ): this {
   943	        if (!this.has(columnSlugA) || !this.has(columnSlugB)) return this
   944	
   945	        const columnA = this.get(columnSlugA)
   946	        const columnB = this.get(columnSlugB)
   947	
   948	        const toleranceA = columnA.tolerance ?? 0
   949	        const toleranceB = columnB.tolerance ?? 0
   950

   212	export function linearInterpolation(
   213	    valuesSortedByTimeAsc: (number | ErrorValue)[],
   214	    timesAsc: Time[],
   215	    context: LinearInterpolationContext,
   216	    start: number = 0,
   217	    end: number = valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length
   218	): void {
   219	    if (!valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length) return
   220	
   221	    let prevNonBlankIndex = -1
   222	    let nextNonBlankIndex = -1
   223	
   224	    for (let index = start; index < end; index++) {
   225	        const currentValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index]
   226	        if (isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(currentValue)) {
   227	            prevNonBlankIndex = index
   228	            continue
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        if (nextNonBlankIndex === -1 || nextNonBlankIndex <= index) {
   232	            nextNonBlankIndex = findIndexFast(
   233	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc,
   234	                (val) => isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(val),
   235	                index + 1,
   236	                end
   237	            )
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        const prevValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[prevNonBlankIndex]
   241	        const nextValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[nextNonBlankIndex]
   242	
   243	        let value
   244	        if (
   245	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(prevValue) &&
   246	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(nextValue)
   247	        ) {
   248	            const distLeft = index - prevNonBlankIndex
   249	            const distRight = nextNonBlankIndex - index
   250	            value =
   251	                (prevValue * distRight + nextValue * distLeft) /
   252	                (distLeft + distRight)
   253	        } else if (
   254	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(prevValue) &&
   255	            context.extrapolateAtEnd
   256	        )
   257	            value = prevValue
   258	        else if (
   259	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(nextValue) &&
   260	            context.extrapolateAtStart
   261	        )
   262	            value = nextValue
   263	        else value = ErrorValueTypes.NoValueForInterpolation
   264	
   265	        prevNonBlankIndex = index
   266	
   267	        valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] = value
   268	    }
   269	}
   270

   272	    valuesSortedByTimeAsc: (number | ErrorValue)[],
   273	    timesAsc: Time[],
   274	    context: ToleranceInterpolationContext,

Now I understand the issue! The problem is in the linear interpolation function. Looking at lines 248-252:

```typescript
const distLeft = index - prevNonBlankIndex
const distRight = nextNonBlankIndex - index
value = (prevValue * distRight + nextValue * distLeft) / (distLeft + distRight)
```

The current implementation uses the **index differences** (`distLeft` and `distRight`) rather than the **actual time differences**. This means it treats all time points as if they are equally spaced, which is incorrect for irregular time intervals.

Let me check how the times are used in the interpolation call:

   190	
   191	export interface LinearInterpolationContext extends InterpolationContext {
   192	    // whether to extrapolate a variable at the start or end, where we cannot do linear interpolation
   193	    // but need to just copy over the first/last value present over to empty fields.
   194	    // e.g. [Error, Error, 2, 3, 4] would become [2, 2, 2, 3, 4] with extrapolateAtStart=true.
   195	    extrapolateAtStart?: boolean
   196	    extrapolateAtEnd?: boolean
   197	}
   198	
   199	export interface ToleranceInterpolationContext extends InterpolationContext {
   200	    timeToleranceForwards: number
   201	    timeToleranceBackwards: number
   202	}
   203	
   204	export type InterpolationProvider<C extends InterpolationContext> = (

Now I need to see what the issue is. Let me check what the `linearInterpolation` function is doing. The issue described in the PR is that when interpolating across irregular time intervals, the interpolation doesn't take spacing into account. Looking at the current implementation, I can see that in lines 248-252, it uses:

```typescript
const distLeft = index - prevNonBlankIndex
const distRight = nextNonBlankIndex - index
value = (prevValue * distRight + nextValue * distLeft) / (distLeft + distRight)
```

However, it's using **array indices** as distances, not **time differences**. This is the root cause of the problem! The interpolation should use the actual time differences between points, not just their positions in the array.

Let me check how the times are passed to this function

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_interpolation_issue.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test script to reproduce the irregular time interval interpolation issue
"""

import sys
import os

# Add testbed to Python path so we can import the modules
sys.path.insert(0, '"'"'/testbed'"'"')

def test_current_linear_interpolation():
    """
    Test the current linear interpolation algorithm to show the issue
    """
    print("Testing current linear interpolation algorithm...")
    
    # Simulate the current behavior - based on array indices
    def current_linear_interpolation(values, times):
        """Current algorithm interpolates based on array positions, not actual time values"""
        result = values.copy()
        
        for i in range(len(values)):
            if values[i] is None:  # Missing value
                # Find previous and next known values
                prev_idx = i - 1
                while prev_idx >= 0 and values[prev_idx] is None:
                    prev_idx -= 1
                
                next_idx = i + 1
                while next_idx < len(values) and values[next_idx] is None:
                    next_idx += 1
                
                if prev_idx >= 0 and next_idx < len(values):
                    # Current bug: using array indices instead of actual time values
                    dist_left = i - prev_idx  # Wrong! Uses index difference, not time difference
                    dist_right = next_idx - i  # Wrong! Uses index difference, not time difference
                    
                    prev_val = values[prev_idx]
                    next_val = values[next_idx]
                    
                    result[i] = (prev_val * dist_right + next_val * dist_left) / (dist_left + dist_right)
                    
                    print(f"  Index {i} (Time {times[i]}): interpolated from index {prev_idx} (time {times[prev_idx]}) and index {next_idx} (time {times[next_idx]})")
                    print(f"    Using distances: left={dist_left}, right={dist_right} (WRONG - based on indices, not actual time)")
                    
        return result
    
    def correct_linear_interpolation(values, times):
        """Correct algorithm interpolates based on actual time values"""
        result = values.copy()
        
        for i in range(len(values)):
            if values[i] is None:  # Missing value
                # Find previous and next known values
                prev_idx = i - 1
                while prev_idx >= 0 and values[prev_idx] is None:
                    prev_idx -= 1
                
                next_idx = i + 1
                while next_idx < len(values) and values[next_idx] is None:
                    next_idx += 1
                
                if prev_idx >= 0 and next_idx < len(values):
                    # Correct: using actual time values for interpolation
                    time_left = times[i] - times[prev_idx]  # Correct time difference
                    time_right = times[next_idx] - times[i]  # Correct time difference
                    
                    prev_val = values[prev_idx]
                    next_val = values[next_idx]
                    
                    result[i] = (prev_val * time_right + next_val * time_left) / (time_left + time_right)
                    
                    print(f"  Index {i} (Time {times[i]}): interpolated from index {prev_idx} (time {times[prev_idx]}) and index {next_idx} (time {times[next_idx]})")
                    print(f"    Using time distances: left={time_left}, right={time_right} (CORRECT - based on actual time differences)")
                    
        return result
    
    # Test case from PR description: Germany with missing values from 1750-1950
    # France has values at 1900, 1910, 1920, 1930, 1940, 1950
    # Germany gets interpolated points at these times
    
    print("\nTest Case 1: Regular intervals (no issue)")
    print("=" * 50)
    times_regular = [1900, 1910, 1920, 1930, 1940, 1950]
    values_germany = [None, None, 50, 60, 70, 80]  # Missing values at 1900, 1910
    
    print("Times:", times_regular)
    print("Values:", values_germany)
    print("\nCurrent algorithm:")
    current_result = current_linear_interpolation(values_germany, times_regular)
    print("Result:", current_result)
    
    print("\nCorrect algorithm:")
    correct_result = correct_linear_interpolation(values_germany, times_regular)
    print("Result:", correct_result)
    print("Note: Both algorithms work fine for regular intervals")
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("\nTest Case 2: Irregular intervals (PROBLEM CASE)")
    print("=" * 50)
    times_irregular = [1750, 1900, 1910, 1920, 1930, 1940, 1950, 2000]
    values_germany_irregular = [10, None, None, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90]  # Long gap from 1750 to 1900
    
    print("Times:", times_irregular)
    print("Values:", values_germany_irregular)
    print("\nCurrent algorithm (WRONG):")
    current_result = current_linear_interpolation(values_germany_irregular, times_irregular)
    print("Result:", current_result)
    
    print("\nCorrect algorithm:")
    correct_result = correct_linear_interpolation(values_germany_irregular, times_irregular)
    print("Result:", correct_result)
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("\nDemonstrating the issue:")
    print("The current algorithm treats the gap from 1750 to 1900 (150 years) as")
    print("equivalent to the gap from 1900 to 1910 (10 years) because it uses")
    print("array index differences instead of actual time differences!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_current_linear_interpolation()'

import { ErrorValueTypes } from "@ourworldindata/core-table"

// Test to reproduce the irregular time interval issue
testIrregularTimeInterpolation()

function testIrregularTimeInterpolation() {
    console.log("Testing linear interpolation with irregular time intervals...")
    console.log("=" .repeat(60))
    
    // Test case 1: Regular intervals (should work fine)
    console.log("\nTest 1: Regular intervals (10-year gaps)")
    const timesRegular = [1900, 1910, 1920, 1930, 1940, 1950]
    const valuesRegular = [
        10, 
        ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder, 
        ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder,
        50, 
        60, 
        70
    ]
    
    console.log("Times:", timesRegular)
    console.log("Values before:", valuesRegular.map(v => v === ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder ? "MISSING" : v))
    
    const regularCopy = [...valuesRegular]
    linearInterpolation(regularCopy, timesRegular, {})
    
    console.log("Values after:", regularCopy)
    
    // Test case 2: Irregular intervals (PROBLEM CASE)
    console.log("\nTest 2: Irregular intervals (PROBLEM CASE)")
    const timesIrregular = [1750, 1900, 1910, 1920, 1930, 1940, 1950]
    const valuesIrregular = [
        10,
        ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder,
        ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder,
        50,
        60,
        70,
        80
    ]
    
    console.log("Times:", timesIrregular)
    console.log("Values before:", valuesIrregular.map(v => v === ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder ? "MISSING" : v))
    
    const irregularCopy = [...valuesIrregular]
    linearInterpolation(irregularCopy, timesIrregular, {})
    
    console.log("Values after:", irregularCopy)
    
    console.log("\n" + "=" .repeat(60))
    console.log("\nISSUE DEMONSTRATION:")
    console.log("The current algorithm uses array indices instead of actual time values.")
    console.log("This causes incorrect interpolation when time intervals are irregular.")
    console.log("For example, the gap from 1750 to 1900 (150 years) is treated the same")
    console.log("as the gap from 1900 to 1910 (10 years) because both are 1 index apart!")
}

// Add a simple linear interpolation that uses time values
function linearInterpolationWithTime(values: (number | any)[], times: number[], context: any) {
    if (!values.length) return
    
    let prevNonBlankIndex = -1
    let nextNonBlankIndex = -1
    
    for (let index = 0; index < values.length; index++) {
        const currentValue = values[index]
        if (currentValue !== ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder) {
            prevNonBlankIndex = index
            continue
        }
        
        if (nextNonBlankIndex === -1 || nextNonBlankIndex <= index) {
            nextNonBlankIndex = index + 1
            while (nextNonBlankIndex < values.length && values[nextNonBlankIndex] === ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder) {
                nextNonBlankIndex++
            }
        }
        
        const prevValue = values[prevNonBlankIndex]
        const nextValue = values[nextNonBlankIndex]
        
        let value
        if (prevValue !== ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder && nextValue !== ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder) {
            // CURRENT BUG: using array indices
            const distLeft = index - prevNonBlankIndex
            const distRight = nextNonBlankIndex - index
            value = (prevValue * distRight + nextValue * distLeft) / (distLeft + distRight)
            
            // CORRECT: using actual time values
            const timeLeft = times[index] - times[prevNonBlankIndex]
            const timeRight = times[nextNonBlankIndex] - times[index]
            const correctValue = (prevValue * timeRight + nextValue * timeLeft) / (timeLeft + timeRight)
            
            console.log(`\nIndex ${index} (Time ${times[index]})`)
            console.log(`  Current (WRONG): uses indices ${prevNonBlankIndex}->${index}->${nextNonBlankIndex}`)
            console.log(`    Result: ${value}`)
            console.log(`  Correct: uses times ${times[prevNonBlankIndex]}->${times[index]}->${times[nextNonBlankIndex]}`)
            console.log(`    Result: ${correctValue}`)
        }
        
        prevNonBlankIndex = index
        values[index] = value
    }
}'

   271	export function toleranceInterpolation(
   272	    valuesSortedByTimeAsc: (number | ErrorValue)[],
   273	    timesAsc: Time[],
   274	    context: ToleranceInterpolationContext,
   275	    start: number = 0,
   276	    end: number = valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length
   277	): void {
   278	    if (!valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length) return
   279	
   280	    let prevNonBlankIndex: number | undefined = undefined
   281	    let nextNonBlankIndex: number | undefined = undefined
   282	
   283	    for (let index = start; index < end; index++) {
   284	        const currentValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index]
   285	        if (isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(currentValue)) {
   286	            prevNonBlankIndex = index
   287	            continue
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        if (
   291	            context.timeToleranceForwards > 0 &&
   292	            nextNonBlankIndex !== -1 &&
   293	            (nextNonBlankIndex === undefined || nextNonBlankIndex <= index)
   294	        ) {
   295	            nextNonBlankIndex = findIndexFast(
   296	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc,
   297	                isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell,
   298	                index + 1,
   299	                end
   300	            )
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        const timeOfCurrent = timesAsc[index]
   304	        const timeOfPrevIndex =
   305	            prevNonBlankIndex !== undefined
   306	                ? timesAsc[prevNonBlankIndex]
   307	                : -Infinity
   308	        const timeOfNextIndex =
   309	            nextNonBlankIndex !== undefined && nextNonBlankIndex !== -1
   310	                ? timesAsc[nextNonBlankIndex]
   311	                : Infinity
   312	
   313	        const prevTimeDiff = Math.abs(timeOfPrevIndex - timeOfCurrent)
   314	        const nextTimeDiff = Math.abs(timeOfNextIndex - timeOfCurrent)
   315	
   316	        if (
   317	            nextNonBlankIndex !== -1 &&
   318	            nextTimeDiff <= prevTimeDiff &&
   319	            nextTimeDiff <= context.timeToleranceForwards
   320	        ) {
   321	            valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] =
   322	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc[nextNonBlankIndex!]
   323	            timesAsc[index] = timesAsc[nextNonBlankIndex!]
   324	        } else if (
   325	            prevNonBlankIndex !== undefined &&
   326	            prevTimeDiff <= context.timeToleranceBackwards
   327	        ) {
   328	            valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] =
   329	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc[prevNonBlankIndex!]
   330	            timesAsc[index] = timesAsc[prevNonBlankIndex!]
   331	        } else
   332	            valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] =
   333	                ErrorValueTypes.NoValueWithinTolerance
   334	    }
   335	}

Now I understand the issue! The problem is in the `linearInterpolation` function in `/testbed/packages/@ourworldindata/core-table/src/CoreTableUtils.ts`. 

Looking at lines 248-249:
```typescript
const distLeft = index - prevNonBlankIndex
const distRight = nextNonBlankIndex - index
```

The function is using **array indices** instead of **actual time values** for the interpolation. This means that a 150-year gap (like 1750-1900) is treated the same as a 10-year gap (like 1900-1910) if they are both separated by one index position in the array.

In contrast, the `toleranceInterpolation` function (lines 313-314) correctly uses actual time differences:
```typescript
const prevTimeDiff = Math.abs(timeOfPrevIndex - timeOfCurrent)
const nextTimeDiff = Math.abs(timeOfNextIndex - timeOfCurrent)
```

Let me fix the `linearInterpolation` function
